)@@G@@          S,H1      A0,COMPKT+1     @F@@@!          COM$P     COMPKT    IE
)@@G@@        . SEND MESSAGE TO CONSOLE   @^@,@!CONT4     TNZ       ROPT@H@,@!IF
)@@G@@          SZ        HEAD,X5           . CLEAR INPUT HEAD IF NOT 'R' OPTIIG
)@@G@@ON    @F@,@!CONT5     LXI       A0,NWDS           . SUBMIT PRINT CONTROLIH
)@@G@@ IMAGE@F@@@,CONT9     LXI       A0,NWDS           . SUBMIT PRINT CONTROLII

)@@G@@CN,X3 @ @@@!          J         LOOP3     @E@@@!DATA      TNZ       KPRIIK

)@@G@@        . WORD COUNT    @ @@@!          LSSL      A0,18     @E@@@!      IO

)@@G@@@E@@@!END       PRTCN$    NOHEAD,1          . TURN OFF HEADING    @E@@@!IS
)@@G@@          PRINT$    MESS1,NMESS1,-1   . PRINT END MESSAGE   @E@@@!      IT
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,POSTPR$       . CLOSE INPUT FILE    @#@@@!          ERIU
)@@G@@R$    @G@@@!          L         X5,(1,0)          . CHECK IF ANY LEFT OVIV
)@@G@@ER HEADINGS @ @@@!          L,U       X1,HDBUFF @ @@@!          L,U     IW
)@@G@@  X2,PRINT  @ @@@!          SZ        KHEAD     @ @@@!          SZ      IX
)@@G@@  BASCII    @ @@@!LOOP5     TNZ       HEAD,X5   @ @@@!          J       IY

)@@G@@          L,S2      A0,HEAD,X5        . GET # OF CHARS@ @@@!          TZJI

)@@G@@       P(1,1) =   FILE $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)                *******  @H@@@QSG
)@@G@@. ********         P(1,2) = ELEMENT $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)               ***SH
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,3) = VERSION $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)      SI

)@@G@@ CALLED              *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$OR  - CALLS 'SOR'      SK
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,1SL
)@@G@@) = (NWDS,ADDR)                              *******  @H@@@Q. ********  SM
